<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодник.html>него́дник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negódnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодник.html>него́дника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодник.html>него́дники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодник.html>него́дников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">него́дница</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> naughty child; rascal; rogue; wretch, mischiefmaker</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодность.html>него́дность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negódnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодность.html>него́дности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодность.html>него́дности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодность.html>него́дностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unfitness, lack of fitness</li>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>--</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a> (15614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negódnyj</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>unfit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребление.html>употребле́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>negódnyj</b> k upotrebléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>unfit</b> for use</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:питье.html>питья́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodá, <b>negódnaja</b> dlja pitʹjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">undrinkable water; water <b>not fit</b> to drink</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">negódnyj k vojénnoj slúžbe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ineligible/<b>unfit</b> for (military) service</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>improper, unsuitable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>negódnyje</b> srédstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>improper/unsuitable</b> means</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попытка.html>попы́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дными</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дствами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popýtka</b> s <b>negódnymi</b> srédstvami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">exercise in futility</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negódnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дных</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дная</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scoundrel, rascal, good-for-nothing, worthless person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ах.html>Ах́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ax, ty <b>negódnyj</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you scoundrel/rascal/good-for-nothing!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:негодовавший.html>негодова́вший</a> (14671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодовавший.html>негодова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negodovávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодовать.html>негодова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negodovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодяй.html>негодя́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negodjáj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодяй.html>негодя́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодяй.html>негодя́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодяй.html>негодя́ев</a></b>)

***негр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a> (4905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">nègre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>не́гра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>не́гры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>не́гров</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Kenyan_man_2.jpg/220px-Kenyan_man_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Kenyan_man_2.jpg/330px-Kenyan_man_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Kenyan_man_2.jpg/440px-Kenyan_man_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="640" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></div></div></div>
<ol><li>black (man); negro</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone who works for peanuts or for nothing, a slave</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ghost writer (usually in the idiom "<a href = vnd.unilang:литературный.html>литерату́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a>")</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The usage of the words <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negritjánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in Russian is <i>generally</i> considered proper and not pejorative/derogative.</li>
<li>Until recently, this word was considered neutral in the Russian usage and preferred over "<a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a>" ("black") and its derivatives.</li>
<li>Due to recent Western influence, some people now avoid the term.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́п</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aráp</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мавр.html>мавр</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mavr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - <i>dated</i></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:африканец.html>африка́нец</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">afrikánec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">а́фро-америка́нец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">áfro-amerikánec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - (literally) African American (neologism, not commonly used)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a> (32115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">negritjánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нок</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a black woman; Negress</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The usage of the word "<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>" or "<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negritjánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>" in Russian is generally not considered pejorative. It is a neutral word in Russian, and is not used derogatively.</li>
<li>Due to Western influence, for political correctness some people avoid the term.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negr</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - black man</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">негритёнок</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negritjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - little black boy</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянский.html>негритя́нский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negritjánskij</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">негрито́с</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negritós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">негрито́ска</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negritóska</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>offensive</i>)</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:негритянский.html>негритя́нский</a> (22051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a hypothetical <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*негритя́нин</span> (whose feminine <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негритянка.html>негритя́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negritjánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is attested) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*негритя́нин</span> contains the same root as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">негритёнок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negritjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (an extended version of the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негр.html>негр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">negr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́нин</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jánin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dalekó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">far, far off, far away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недалеко.html>недалеко́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedalekó</span>)
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко́</a></b>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недействительный.html>недействи́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedejstvítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> invalid, void, null
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недействительный.html>недействи́тельным</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ <b>nedejstvítelʹnym</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invalidate; nullify</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> past its expiry/expiration term, expired</li>
<li>untrue</li></ol>

***неделя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неделя</a> (397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">недѣлꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedělja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Sunday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*neděľa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Sunday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">де́л-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dél-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">work</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally used to mean Sunday, the day of rest.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedélja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ль</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>week
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́лю</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>nedélju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">per week</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na próšloj <b>nedéle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">last week</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na étoj <b>nedéle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this week</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущий.html>бу́дущей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na búduščej <b>nedéle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">next week</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sunday</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недержание.html>недержа́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nederžánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недержание.html>недержа́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недержание.html>недержа́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недержание.html>недержа́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брый</a> (6452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóbryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedóbryj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unkind, hostile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nedóbroje</b> čúvstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hostile/ill feeling</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вства</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pitátʹ <b>nedóbryje</b> čúvstva (k)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bear ill will <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">towards</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bad, wicked, evil
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весть.html>весть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nedóbraja</b> vestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bad news</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nedóbroj</b> pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">of cursed memory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>nedóbryj</b> čas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in an evil hour; on a black day</span></div></dd>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоверие.html>недове́рие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedovérije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоверие.html>недове́рия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоверие.html>недове́рия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоверие.html>недове́рий</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льство</a> (6823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovólʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedovólʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>discontent, dissatisfaction, displeasure; resentment</li></ol>
